<Author>tgonzalez0406
<Content>Great Location! We stayed at Hotel Milano the night before cruising on the Carnival Liberty. This hotel is right in the heart of San Juan and only about 5 blocks or so from the port. You have easy access to food and everything else in the city. They were also very reasonably priced compared to the other hotels in the area. It is a very basic hotel and if you are looking for fancy this is not it. Its great for one night. You also want to make sure you get a room in the front. There is a club next to the hotel and you can hear the music from it in the rooms in the back. Other than that great stay. We had the continental breakfast the next morning which was only $6.00 a piece. There is also a Mcdonalds and Burger King if you dont want that. There is a great Spanish food resteraunt called Raizes a few blocks away where the food is incredible.

<Author>BuckeyeTraveler68
<Content>Small and Intimate. Great Location! We stayed at Hotel Milano the day prior to our cruise. The definite pluses were the location and the friendliness of the staff. At check out time, they would store your bags which gave us time to tour the town without worrying about what to do with our bags. Even at the end of our stay, the manager loaded our luggage onto the cab for us. The rooms were definitely small and vary amongst other rooms. We ended up with a corner room which was significantly smaller but the same price as the other larger rooms our friends had. I was able to note this to management and they gave me a reduction in the price. In addition, do ask for a room in the middle of the hotel and not an outside room. It was very noisy during the middle of the night with all the bars close by. Overall for a one night stay it was very nice because everything was within walking distance. The only area that wasn't close by were the casinos which you would need to take a short cab ride to.

<Author>ewpeetz
<Content>Perfect Location! We stayed at the Hotel Milano after reading the reviews in Trip Advisor, and we were extremely pleased. We arrived after a weeks cruise on a Sunday before noon, and the staff were very gracious, checking our luggage until rooms were available. We set off from the hotel to explore Old San Juan, and found it was pefectly located to see the old city. After exploring the streets, doing some shopping, eating lunch and touring the Fort, we returned to the hotel to check in and take a nap. Our room was located on the 4th floor, and the elevator was more that adequate to take us and all our luggage upstairs. Our room had no regular windows, just glass block windows located high up on the wall from which we couldn't look through. No matter, this hotel is clean, the bed and bathroom were comfortable and pretty, (loved the cut-linen shower curtain), the fridge was big enough to hold plenty of wine, etc. We heard no noise from the street or the rest of the hotel. The front desk staff were especially helpful, and advised us about cabs etc. for our early morning flight. It did take less than 5 minutes for the taxi to arrive in the morning, as they said it would. This hotel is very reminiscent of European hotels we have visited, (however the rooms at the Milano were larger than many European hotels) and I would highly recommend it to anyone looking an excellent value in Old San Juan.

<Author>Girl_Traveller11
<Content>Nice Hotel, GREAT Location! The Hotel Milano in Old San Juan is a great place to stay, especially for the location. The hotel is located right in the heart of Old San Juan and is in walking distance to all the sights and all the restaurants and bars in the area. The hotel itself is nice (if not a little dated). The people at the front desk were friendly and are more than happy to hold luggage or call you a cab. Surprisingly, the hotel is quiet at night. We had no problem with noise inside or outside of the hotel while we were sleeping. The rooms are clean (the carpet is a little old) and they come with a cable tv and refrigerator. The price was pretty good when we went also. If you are looking for a nice little hotel where you don't have to worry about transportation, this would be a great choice.

<Content>Milano Was Marvelous! We stayed at Hotel Milano for one night (pre-cruise) in September 2008. As advised by many reviewers, we asked for and received a room at the back of the hotel which was very quiet. We were very pleased with our choice of Hotel Milano! The hotel has a very nice exterior and lobby. The staff were friendly, helpful, and spoke excellent English. The room was very much like a European hotel room 鈥?small but perfectly adequate. Our accommodations were very clean and comfortable. The hotel is perfectly situated for exploring Old San Juan. It is also in the heart of the shopping/dining district with lots of restaurants to choose from within easy walking distance. The hotel鈥檚 rooftop restaurant is a lovely, relaxing spot for sipping a morning coffee and getting a panoramic view of the old city. The restaurant is open for breakfast only 鈥?it is a continental breakfast which costs $5 per person. Our criteria for a hotel are: clean, safe, comfortable, reasonably priced. Hotel Milano met every criteria and we were delighted with our choice. We would definitely stay here again even for an extended stay. Before you book this hotel, be honest with yourself about what you鈥檙e looking for in a hotel. For the price, you can鈥檛 beat this hotel for a clean, comfortable room that is quiet and secure. As other reviewers have pointed out, if you鈥檙e looking for a large hotel with lots of luxurious extras, this is not the hotel for you. You鈥檙e just not going to find it at this price in Old San Juan.

<Author>Sunshine02120
<Content>Not a luxury hotel, but nice This isn't a luxury hotel and doesn't have a ton of amenities, but it is very nice. We felt that it was our home away from home. It's within walking distance of everything- museums, forts, shops, eateries etc. You even have a trolley stop a block from the hotel, which is convenient for those who don't want to walk to the forts. Also convenient, if you like to shop or want to rest a bit throughout the day- after shopping, we would stop in to rest and drop off bags and after 15 mins or so we'd take off again.I don't know about other posts on here, but our room was clean when we arrived. We got clean towels every day and our room was clean when we got back in the afternoon. If you are used to the Ritz or HIlton, or expect a room like theirs, then this may not be the place for you. Quick check-in/out process.There was a small refrigerator in our room, which was great. A small microwave would've been convenient to heat our leftovers for a late snack, asbit seems that there weren't any eateries that would deliver. (According to one staff member.) Sometimes we'd want to eat something around 11pm and most places were closing or closed. I do have to say that the elevator is a bit scary; we got scared every time it stopped. We didn't go to the restaurant (Panorama), therefore I cannot comment on that. The only thing I know is that it is $5.00 pp, plus tax. (Obviously)The staff was friendly (except for one person who seemed a bit into self) but besides that, excellent service from the rest! We were always greeted by these individuals who called our taxi  even called a few tour companies to try to get us on one. (Thanks!) We had great chats with these individuals and they always managed to say hello and smile. I would stay here again. I am a simple gal who likes the simple things in life.

<Author>quasan
<Content>Charming  With the help of TripAdvisor, I found out about this great hotel in San Juan. The staff was friendly, the rooms made me feel like I was right at home, and the location was more than perfect. It's on a cute, cobblestone street with lots of great restaurants and entertainment just steps away.The hotel is not loaded with amenities, but definitely has all the basics you would need to feel more than comfortable. If you plan on exploring the city and just being at the hotel to take a siesta and sleep at night, then Hotel Milano is a great choice. I experienced absolutely no noise pollution as some of the other reviews mentioned. My only complaints were that the shower stall was not totally clean and some of the cereal boxes offered for breakfast were expired. Overall, I recommend Hotel Milano and would stay there again during my next visit to PR.

<Author>diatwo
<Content>Great location, basic ammenities Hotel Milano is more of a place to sleep than a destination itself. Do not expect to be wowed by the hotel decor, service, or ammenities. Hotel Milano offers clean, basic rooms. Its strength is its location in the heart of Old San Juan, just steps from the best restaurants, bars, and nightlife. If you plan on spending signficant time in your hotel room or are seeking a nice view, upscale furnishings, or a romantic atmosphere, this is not the hotel for you. If you want a place to store your luggage while you explore the city and its surroundings and a safe, convenient place to sleep at night, Hotel Milano is perfect. Due to its location in the center of the best nightlife, it can be loud late in the evenings. The quietest rooms are in the back of the hotel. I stayed for one Saturday night and heard the bass from the clubs until around 4am. However, it wasn't loud enough to really disturb my sleep.

<Author>kristumz
<Content>Great price, great location, nice and clean We have stayed at Hotel Milano twice in the past few years. It has an ideal location in historic Old San Juan. You can walk to the incredible old forts, shore side walking paths, and fantastic restaurants. You can also walk to the Bacardi Distillery if you want to. It is in a very nice, safe neighborhood where residents and families are out in the street at night chatting, relaxing, and buying pina coladas outdoors from the corner vendors. There are flowing vines and wrought iron balconies lining the streets, and festivals and parties with traffic routes closed off at night. The hotel itself is not fancy, but clean, with a helpful, friendly staff. The price is right, too, starting at $85 to be in the center of town.It is not very near the big resort/beach areas, but I prefer to go to one of the outlying islands for beach activities, where they aren't overrun with tourists and crowds. Old San Juan is interesting and beautiful for its history and ambience.

<Author>spandrelina
<Content>The cockroach on the wall was the least of our problems... I grew up on the island and have always known this hotel to be a lovely spot in the heart of Old San Juan. Something must have happened in the past few years...No one helped us with our luggage- even though the bellhop was hanging out in the lobby speaking to the desk clerk. We also arrived to find the famous Panorama restaurant on the top floor closed until further notice. The Panorama, by the way, is also the location of the internet hotspot on the property.The elevator jolts so strongly when it reaches its destination that you desperately grab for something- anything- to hold on to; and it never gets any better.There is a stale carpet smell that permeates the entire place, and upon entering our room our hearts sank. This was not like any of the rooms pictured online- everything was rusty and smelly, there was barely any room to walk, every surface was sticky, the mattress must have been at least ten years old and it showed- the pillows were flat, the blankets had an odor to them, etc. We went to the lobby and requested a room change and were told that nothing could be done, but that they would refund our next two nights stay if we wished. (We had paid for the full three nights months ago). Funnily enough, the lady at the front desk did not seemed surprised at all that we were disappointed with our room- as if this were a common event for her. We decided to toughen up and stay through the night. We watched all of the six channels available on the grimy tv set and laughed at the fact that there was no phone book available (plus even local calls are thirty cents a minute) but there were tons of pamphlets on catholicism on the dresser (all marked as please do not remove from room) The next morning we woke up and there was a cockroach on our wall, just casually traipsing by. Then we headed out to beautiful Old San Juan after waiting for the elevator with a professional. (nope, not kidding).If you are on a super tight budget and want to stay in the heart of Old San Juan ( a definite bonus) then take this place into consideration. This place can definitely be sold as a motel, but that is about it. Consider the HoJo around the corner. They were kind enough to refund our money, however- I genuinely hope that our stay was atypical...

<Author>kevart
<Content>Noisy  We read the reviews and Hotel Milano sounded acceptable for a short stay in San Juan. The rooftop resturant was a big draw.The rooftop resturant has been closed since December, the free contentinental breakfast is now $5.00 per person. Although we were told none of this on the telephone, we would have been OK if we had been given a room we could sleep in. Our room (303) vibrated with noise from a compressor of some sort outside the window. I asked for a room which was not next to the compressor and was given the key to 403. As this was right above 303, it also vibrated. But, even worse, when I first flipped on the light, a cockroach came scurrying out of the fake plant on the table. I told the clerk about the roach, he offered me the key to room 304. We spent the night in 304. The room has no windows, just some glass blocks near the ceiling. The room vibrated and rumbled all night long. It was loud. The walls were vibrating so much that the framed pictures on the wall vibrated - adding even more noise. The dresser vibrated against the wall- more noise. . Sleep was absolutely impossible. The staff were polite and did alllow us to check out the next morning (a day early) without paying the usual $50.00 fee. All three of the rooms we were shown were completely unacceptable, I would not recoment this hotel to anyone.

<Author>sarahrick
<Content>Great, unless you plan to spend time in your room We stayed two nights in Hotel Milano last week. For the price and location, this is the place to stay in Old San Juan. Very reasonable (almost cheap!) price, fantastic location - Fortaleza street is where it's at for shopping and restaurant selection. Be ready for street noise/music into the wee hours if you have a room on the street side. The people at the desk were very friendly, professional, and helpful. The $5 breakfast was a good deal but nothing special. The thing we didn't like was that the rooms were small, old, and well, not very nice to hang out in at all. We were often tired from shopping and wanted a place to just hang out and read and relax. This is when we wished we had spend the extra money to stay someplace nicer, like the Gallery Inn. But if you plan to spend all of your time in the streets, shops, and restaurants - go for Hotel Milano!  
<Date>May 1, 2008

<Author>Edie_and_Erno
<Content>The Hotel Milano, Old San Juan, PR, was a delight. My husband and I stayed 8 nights at the Hotel Milano, 307 Fortaleza Street, Old San Juan, Puerto Rico, and it was everything we needed. The location was right in the heart of Old San Juan on a street with some of the best restaurants in the historic section, between the two forts, and within easy walking distance of all the sights. A generous breakfast, included in the price of the room, was served with Latin music from a jukebox on a roof from which we had a beautiful view. The room was clean and comfortable and the bathroom was always kept well-stocked with toiletpaper, facial tissues, soap, and shampoo. The tv in our room had good reception, so we were able to keep up with the news. At the computer in the lobby we printed the boarding passes for the return flight. The entire staff, the housekeepers, concierge, and breakfast-hosts, were pleasant, conscientious, and helpful.

<Author>LasMananitas
<Content>Very nice, but you might want earplugs The Hotel Milano's location is a real plus during the day because Old San Juan's historic sites and restaurants are all within walking distance. Unfortunately street noise becomes a problem at night if you book a room facing the street. We booked over the phone and were given the choice of a front room with a window, or an inside room without windows. I picked a front room, thinking a windowless room would be claustrophobic... but now I realize it would have the advantage of being quiet!Otherwise, the staff is friendly, our room was clean and comfortable, and we appreciated the mini-fridge. I'd stay there again... I'd just pick up a pair of those foam earplugs at the drugstore first!

<Author>MargaretGranada
<Content>Excellent small hotel in an ideal locationl This is a lovely small hotel with personalised service and excellent value for money. We spent one night in January and two nights in February at the Hotel Milano in San Juan. The hotel is situated in an ideal location, right in the centre of the old town and right next to some really good restaurants. The rooms are comfortable, nicely decorated and have efficient air-conditioning units. On our first night we stayed in one of the rooms which overlooked the street outside and we didn't find it at all noisy, contrary to some other reports we had read. The reception staff were extremely helpful and efficient, particularly Laura. Breakfast is served in the restaurant at the top of the building, where there is also an open patio area with views over the roof tops. Breakfast consists of hot rolls, croissants or apple turnovers, fruit, cereal, juice, tea and coffee. The restaurant at the moment is only open for breakfast. We had two wonderful dinners at the nearby Marmalade Restaurant (pacific rim with a touch of Iberia) and the Tantra (Indo-Latino Cuisine), where there was also an extensive list of exotic martinis. We will definitely stay at this hotel again on our next trip to San Juan.  
<Date>Mar 8, 2008

I met the owner and got chatting. My wife and I ended up going out for drinks and appetizers with him (and he picked up the check which was most generous). If you get a chance to chat to him, it is really time well spent as he truly is a good person and we are very glad to be giving him our business.We had breakfast included in our room rate and it was simple but great. The breakfast staff was again a very friendly crew and helpful, interested in what our plans for the day was.This is the only hotel in Old San Juan we will use. Easy to get to and easy to get around walking. Great location for basing one self from.

<Author>Jim_and_Barbie
<Content>Bad sleep, good location Another review warned that some rooms do not have any windows, so when I booked my room I was sure to request a room with a window. Perhaps that was a mistake. Even though we were on the 4th floor, the noise from the busy street in front of the hotel was too loud to allow a good night's sleep. We were there on a Saturday night, and the loud noise from the party crowd on the street lasted until well past 3 AM.I don't know if the hotel has rooms with windows on the back of the hotel away from the street. If so, I would ask for one of those. Otherwise, I would probably opt for a room without windows, or try a different hotel.Parking is a bit of a hassle, so if you will be staying at this hotel at the beginning of your trip, consider renting your car on the day you leave the old San Juan area. If you will be staying here at the end of your trip, turn in your rental car first, then take a cab to the hotel from the rental car place. Then just take a cab to the airport on the day you leave. That's what we ended up doing, and it worked out well. Old San Juan is small enough so you can just walk. No need for a car, particularly since the parking is expensive and 2 blocks away. The hotel's location is excellent for walking around old San Juan.

<Author>1allsop
<Content>While not being exceptional it does not deserve the bad reviews We were a bit concerned when we chose the Hotel Milano in San Juan. Although chose might be the wrong term as all other Hotels were booked out and we had no other choice. Admittedly, we were slightly concerned as there were many negative reviews. For this reason we were expecting an old, bad place. Not so! It is clean and the staff is mostly friendly. We were pleasantly surprised. Futhermore, the location is exceptional: literally in the middle of old San Juan. Do not expect flashy rooms with a magnficient view though: our room had very small windows with a view to brick wall (note that almost all rooms share the same dull view), but its reviews on tripadvisor are way below what it deserves. The only negative aspect is that at night, and especially during weekends, the nearby clubs are quite noisy and you can hear the music. Nothing major - especially if you have earplugs. All in all I would definitely recommend it and I think it deserves a rating of four, especially if consider its location and its extremely good price.

<Author>SE53
<Content>Service beyond compare Just spent the last two nights of a 10-day Puerto Rico vacation at Hotel Milano. Owner Juan San Emeterio was clearly the highpoint of not only our stay there, but of our entire vacation. He is gracious, attentive, generous, and utterly delightful. Our room was clean, quiet, simple; bed was very comfortable. I would definitely return, but would not stay in the same room due to its only two extremely tiny windows. (To the hotel's credit, the clerk who took the booking mentioned small windows in the only room he said was free; but these were unimaginably tiny - perhaps 10 inches square - high up just below the ceiling. Other guests mentioned their windows were fine.) Only other room problem we encountered was that there was no way to control the AC until we asked, but then we were given one of (only) two existing remotes from the front desk, which worked fine. We loved being able to have continental breakfast outside on the rooftop, although encroaching development is fast shrinking the view of the city. The evening restaurant grill is no longer in operation, but there are so many great restaurants worth exploring within even just a block of the hotel that we had no shortage of great dining experiences. Juan also gave us excellent recommendations, so each of our meals in Old San Juan were really great. The hotel location is superb for walking around Old San Juan. And when we wanted to go outside the city, Juan facilitated trips to the produce market, the Santurce Art Museum (beautiful!),etc., including to the airport when we departed. I can't wait to return to San Juan, to bask in the warmth of the city as well as the warmth that emanates from Juan San Emeterio and Hotel Milano.

<Author>RDPWiltshire_England
<Content>Good value accommodation for old San Juan A good value, clean, friendly independent hotel right in the heart of old San Juan. The hotel is nothing fancy, but does what it does very well indeed. The the public areas, the bedroom and the linen were comfortable, well-maintained and clean. Our room only had high-level windows with a view (if you are tall) of blank walls and air-conditioning units, but that didn't matter to us - we were out and about most of the time.The roof terrace breakfast area was very pleasant with views (restricted) in all directions, but was not accessible directly from the elevator (a short flight of steps). The breakfast was included and was fairly basic, but adequate. We didn't try the restaurant.We found the hotel a perfect base for exploring old San Juan on foot before joining a cruise ship. If you have mobility problems neither the hotel nor the area are ideal. The hotel is on a very narrow and congested one-way street. If you expect to park a rental car anywhere nearby... forget it! Even the taxis have to block the traffic to pick or drop off. Being in the old town the taxi ride from the airport will be slightly further than to the main beach hotels, but still only came to $20 for two people with a case each.We liked it and would stay there again.

<Author>No-Doz
<Content>Rooms without Windows Many rooms at the Hotel Milano have NO windows. None, they are like closets. I reserved directly through the hotel and neither their website or any of the communications I had regarding my reservation made any mention that the $155 room I had booked was window-free. I would have never reserved the room and in fact would have paid more for even a sliver of real light. It was really claustrophobic.Of course by the time I was in, the place was full - as was San Juan - so I had no choice. A sympathetic staff person said it was the policy to only tell people their room would not have a window if they asked. When was the last time you thought to ask: will my room have a window?Other complaints (which I would normally let go, but am willing to list given the hotel's unethical policies regarding giving guests full information about their rooms):1) The advertised wi-fi doesn't always work. Another guest and I couldn't get the system to give our laptops IP addresses to connect.2) Breakfast only lasts until 10am, not uncommon but with a noon check-out time you'd think staff would let guests know the hours, especially given the relatively generous check-out time. I found no hours posted in the room (I did find some lights so I could see in the room...)3) Also minor but worth noting: the TV channel selection is woeful. C-SPAN but not network stations that would show things like the NFL during playoff season.All-in-all, I wish I could have liked the Hotel Milano but the egregious policies regarding the sale of windowless rooms plus the general lack of comfort means I can't. At least I wasn't tempted NOT to spend every waking moment outside of the hotel enjoying San Juan.

<Author>SV_and_JM
<Content>Comfortable hotel in Old San Juan This is a comfortable and friendly hotel right in the centre of Old San Juan. We originally booked for one night, but decided to stay a second and the receptionist helpfully rearranged other bookings so that we could stay in the same room. We had a room at the back of the hotel, with a window which looked out onto a boring back yard and other buildings, but it meant we could sleep with the window open without being unduly troubled by noise. Rooms are clean and pleasant, if nothing out of the ordinary.The rooftop restaurant is a lovely spot for breakfast, with an indoor and an outdoor section. The breakfast is fairly basic. Excellent coffee, but tea is the usual weak affair that has to be specially requested (Oh well, if we British must travel abroad, what can we expect ....?) It is a pity the restaurant now seems to be permanently closed in teh evenings. But there are restaurants all around, so it doesn't really matter. And the location is so convenient for sight-seeing; you can easily pop back during the day if you want to.We paid $115 for a double room which seemed good value and I would certainly consider staying there again if we ever return to San Juan.

<Author>Seala
<Content>Decent hotel but nothing special After reading reviews on trip advisor, we decided to stay at the Hotel Milano during a recent trip to Puerto Rico but was slightly disappointed with the hotel. While it has a cute lobby and is in a good location (though a little noisy because it is on a busy main street) the rooms did not have much character. They were clean but very plain and basic. Some of the rooms do not have windows so make sure you ask about that. The ones that do face the street and can be a bit noisy. The breakfast was very plain and nothing special as well. The staff were friendly and fairly helpful. Overall, I found the hotel to be just ok - clean and basic- so if that's all you're looking for it could be a good choice. I think it is overpriced for what you get unless you can get a very good rate. I stay at many small botique hotels and know what to expect but found this too be a little too best western for what we were expecting when paying close to $200 a night. Unfortunately I don't know that there are any better choices in Old San Juan unless you are willing to spend much more for a room.

<Author>prkranger
<Content>great location,price and staff Great hotel for a good price and great location. My wife and I stayed overnight after our cruise ended in Puerto Rico. The hotel is a short walk from the pier and about a 15 minutes taxi ride to the airport.The hotel staff was friendly and courteous and allowed us to leave our luggage in a safe area as we arrived at 10:30am and check-in wasn't till 3:00 pm. This hotel is centrally located in old San Juan making everything within walking distance. There are shops up and down the street if you want to get a taste of the Puerto Rican culture.We happened to book the last available room for the night and it was in the front or street side of the hotel. I would suggest you book early and get a room in the back. I don't think this is a problem unique to the Hotel Milano as the streets are narrow in old San Juan with lots of vehicle traffic.Also there was a large festival in the town square of Old san Juan during our stay which may have affected he noise factor.My wife and walked through the streets at night and felt safe and the locals are very friendly with directions. The breakfast in the morning is adequate and the manager is a very nice fellow.I was very pleased with the Hotel Milano and if you check prices for other hotels in the area they are very reasonable. I would definitely recommend this hotel. ]

<Author>VAWiski
<Content>Good Value Great location. We stayed one night prior to a cruise and five nights after the cruise. Good value, great location for touring Old San Juan. Roof top restaurant is closed and will probably stay closed. I expect the competition of the many great restaurants within walking distance (everything in Old Town is within walking distance) is too much to overcome. The restaurant is open for a modest but adequate breakfast every day - which you may supplemented by a visit to any one of several good bakeries nearby (if you can afford to put on a few more pounds). Good WiFi connection on the roof too. The daytime desk clerk is helpful but the porter/breakfast manager is especially cordial and will be a great information resource. On street parking is available if you are extremely lucky. Three nearby garages charge significantly different overnight rates. Check with the hotel to see which is currently the most reasonable. The Bacardi rum factory tour is worth doing even if you are not into rum. Take the ferry from Pier 2 to add to the enjoyment.

<Author>k1nu
<Content>Great place to stay in Old San Juan Like a lot of others, we needed somewhere to stay overnight in/near Old San Juan prior to our cruise ship departure. Based on reviews from this web site, we chose Hotel Milano. The rates were great, the staff was very friendly, and the room was perfect. We enjoyed dinner and breakfast on the rooftop restaurant, and walked from the hotel to the shopping district and El Morro, before departing that evening. The hotel provides a secure place to leave your luggage for the day, the cruise dock is walking distance. This hotel is NOT a Westin or Marriott resort - don't expect that. It's a quaint little inn, great for a short stay and perfect for those cruising from San Juan. I'd stay there again. One recommendation (which we did): get a room with a window if you can. Some rooms are interior.

<Author>inspire7656
<Content>Hotel Milano Rocks! I recently had the pleasure of staying at the Hotel Milano in San Juan and everything was beyond my expectations for an enjoyable trip. I even had the room with no real windows, but glass that allowed sunlight in! The price was right, the air cooled, the room very clean and updated, the tv worked great, and the refrigerator was a bonus. Free breakfast in the morning, and great food for dinner if desired. You even get as much free bottled water as desired! I love the rooftop restaurant as you can be under a canopy overlooking the bay or inside the airconditioned part of the restaurant. To round out the experience, the hotel is very centrally located to catch all the sights. A lovely place and the owner is very nice too. I definitely highly recommend the Hotel Milano as a place to stay in San Juan. I know I'll return!

<Author>nothintolose
<Content>It served it's purpose We stayed here for one night during our brief stay in San Juan. The hotel was fine for what we were looking for. It was not anything fancy, but it served it's purpose.The staff was very nice and helpful from check in to check out and afterwards because we left our bags there while we walked around Old San Juan till we had to leave for the airport.The Panorama Restaurant on top of the hotel had good food and nice service for dinner. The continental breakfast left alot to be desired though. We reserved a room facing the street by accident because my other half misunderstood me when (after reading here) I told him not to get a room on the street. It wasn't that bad though, I was woken up around 1:30 in the morning by a car going by playing exceptionally loud music but never heard all of the street noise everyone is mentioning. I have stayed in the French Quarter off of Bourbon Street and heard more noise than I heard at this hotel.The room was just an average room, but it served it's purpose. We were not expecting a 5 star hotel though. The a/c was HOT when we got in the room, but when we called down to the desk, they told us we needed to pick up the remote to change the temperature. Once we did that, it was fine. The room had cooled off by the time we came back from dinner.We would definitely stay there again as it is in a VERY convenient location in Old San Juan. We walked to all three forts from there and all around town. The bus goes by it as well. The manager recommended The Parrot Club to us for lunch and we were VERY happy with his recommendation. Both of the men that manned the front desk were extremely pleasant and helpful.Hope this helps.ElizabethNew Orleans, LA

<Author>ociene
<Content>Great stay We had a great stay at the Hotel Milano. For the price and location, I think it was definitely worth it and would recommend it to friends. It's not fancy, but we thought the decorations and cleanliness and general comfort were just fine. The rooms are simple but we were happy with ours. We took the advice of one of the reviews here and stayed in a rear-facing room, so we had no problems with noise. The windows are incredibly tiny but at least gave a little light, and the room size was fine. The staff were very nice, always happy to hold our key when we'd go for a run (and then laugh with us when we came back very humid) or greet us at breakfast. Breakfast was simple but there was plenty of food and the restaurant atmosphere is nice. The best part of the hotel, in my opinion, is its location. Where you'd be paying a Lot more for a different hotel in old San Juan, here you saved the money and were still in the thick of it. There is lots of shopping on or just off Forteleza street, and lots of bars and restaurants and the casino are about a 10 minute walk. The bar where pina coladas were invented is a 10 minute walk up Forteleza. You can walk easily to El Morro or San Cristobal or explore the north shore. It's a little under a 2 mile walk to the nearest beach. The cruise port and lots of little shopping stands along the south shore are really close, too. Get a good map and enjoy wandering through the city!  
<Date>Jul 28, 2007

<Author>TravelinGatorFans
<Content>Not what I'd call upscale at all We booked one night at the Hotel Milano based on the reviews we'd read here, and I was sorely disappointed. It was hardly upscale (as described on its own webpage), nor as nice as I'd been led to believe it would be from the other reviews. I actually, for a while, wondered if there were two Hotel Milanos and we'd somehow wound up at the wrong one.The staff, from what we saw of them, were pleasant enough. The room, though, was way too warm (the A/C barely brought it down to a comfortable level), the bed was too soft and the pillows too hard. The hallways and stairways looked very worn and shabby.Our biggest problem was at night. Our room faced the street, and we can tell you exactly what time the bars in San Juan close on Saturday nights: 4am. The noise was unbelievable, and kept us awake most of the night. We tried to make light of it and joke about it, but I would definitely not stay there again because of it.The hotel's restaurant atop the hotel offered a nice view of Old San Juan. The dinner we had there that night was actually quite good. The breakfast, though, was another disappointment. Very little in the way of variety, even for a Continental-style breakfast.As I said, I was very surprised to have this experience after all the glowing reviews I'd read about it. Oh well... Live and learn, I guess.

<Author>cltravelers2
<Content>Great location, comfortable rooms On our first night in Puerto Rico, we stayed in Old San Juan. When we arrived we found that a street festival was taking place that weekend on Fortaleza Street, including the block in front of Hotel Milano. So needless to say, this hotel is in a great location. There are a bunch of trendy restaurants within a block (highly recommend The Parrot Club -- amazing mojtos and food) and you can walk to both forts and all of the sights of Old San Juan from the hotel. The location can't be beat. The rooms were very comfortable and the desk staff very helpful. Our only complaint was the continental breakfast, which was on par with something like a Holiday Inn in the U.S. I think we just expected something with more of a local feel. All in all, for the price, Hotel Milano is highly recommended.

<Author>vee777
<Content>Nice if you don't have a rental car I took a five-day trip around Puerto Rico staying in Old San Juan two nights. When I drove up to check into the hotel, I had to move the barracades from in front of the hotel to parallel park since it is a narrow one-way street. When I was going up to my room, the receptionist informed me that I had to move my car to public parking. It was an inconvenience that they did not offer a service man to do that. The last thing that anyone wants to do is drop off your luggage walk half a mile each way and then get ready to go out. The parking garages that are available are pretty expensive. The cheapest that was around was $1 for the first hour and $.65 for each additional hour. This adds up if you are staying for more than one night. The hotel itself has a nice appearance. There wasn't a window to look out of due to being in squeezed in by buisnesses on both sides. The room was clean and spacious, but the air-conditioner was a bit squeeky. It quieted down a bit after being turned on for several hours.The hotel is obviously located in a convenient location. There are many restaurants, shops and bars close by. Nice location, a bit overpriced $149+tax, to not include parking somehow. You will enjoy this hotel if you are just staying in Old San Juan.

<Author>mkchaffin
<Content>The Milano was OK We just returned from a two night stay at Hotel Milano. When we checked in the receptionist at the front desk was not too friendly. However we never did see him again, and from then on they all were friendly. To our disappointment there was no internet connection in the room. We were told that there was a connection in the restaurant, but it was open only certain hours. When we opened the door to the room, it had a musty smell, but the A/C was on. We asked someone about it, and was told that a remote was needed, which was brought to us. The room was OK but we thought it would at least have windows--it only had three small glass sqaures at the top to let in a little light. The restaurant, Panorama, was supposed to have a view, but there was a tall building under construction blocking most of the view of the water. The black bean soup was delicious. The best thing about this hotel is the location. It is very conveniently located to everything in Old San Juan.

<Author>ksakmorris
<Content>Good Experience at Hotel Milano We just stayed for one night at Hotel Milano after being on Culebra for a week. We were a large group and had 3 rooms. We found the Milano to suit our needs well. The front desk staff were very friendly and helpful at check-in. One of the rooms in our group had been booked separately, so they didn't know we were together. They made sure to put us on the same floor, which we really appreciated. We were in the front of the building and yes, there is some noise, but the a/c blocks most of it out. The beds are very soft and bouncy, so some people may not like that, others may love it. Rooms are small, but very clean. The rooftop restaurant was nice and had a good view. Breakfast, as has been said, is basic, but adequate to start the day.We only had 2 problems. The a/c in our friends' room got very cold, to the point of being too cold to sleep. The a/c is not adjustable, so it was that or open the windows and have the noise of the street. The 2nd thing is more of an issue than a problem. We wanted to print out our boarding passes for our flights home, but they didn't seem too eager to do this. After asking a couple times, we finally got to go into the office and a gentleman working there had to stop working on his computer so I could print out our passes. He was not too friendly about this, but I don't know how much I can blame him---we were disrupting his work! It would be great if they had a small business area where this could be done without disrupting any of the employees.Other than that, it was a great stay! We would definitely return!

<Author>heypaula717
<Content>Pros and Cons We stayed at the Hotel Milano in Feb. 2007 - 1 night pre-cruise and 1 night post-cruise. The main advantage of the hotel, in my opinion, was its location. It was great to be within walking distance of so many of the sights in Old San Juan. Also, there is a free bus to El Morro, which we took advantage of while there. The hotel is also within a few blocks of 2 of the main cruise piers. Unfortunately, our ship departed from the third! However, it was a short taxi drive, and not a problem.We booked a room in the front of the hotel, as we had read that the rear rooms were smaller and some lacked windows that could be opened, which sounded a little claustrophobic to me. The room itself was quite adequate and clean, though a bit small, as we expected in an older hotel such as this. Our main problem was the noise from the street, which continued until 4AM both nights we stayed. Part of this was our own fault, as we left the windows open. However, the air-conditioner was just 'On or off' - with it off, the room was very hot, but with it on it was frigid - so we opted to leave it off. It may have helped with the noise to have the unit turned on, but I'm not sure we had enough blankets for that!The restaurant on the roof was very nice, although the views are not as scenic as the photos, as there is a lot of construction in the area. The food was good, and so was the service - so it was enjoyable. However, the complimentary morning breakfast was very minimal - beverages, packaged donuts, and boxed cereals. It was a start to the day, though - and we found several nice restauarants nearby for a more substantial meal.I would probably not stay here again, but I would recommend it to anyone wanting a reasonably priced comfortable room in Old San Juan. The staff is friendly and helpful, and it's a great location as a base for sightseeing.  
<Date>Feb 26, 2007

<Author>ladewig
<Content>Very disappointed We stayed for one night (on a Thurs) prior to our cruise. The best feature of this hotel is its location right in the heart of Old San Juan. It was within a few blocks walking distance of a great restaurant (The Parrot Club). However, the small size of the hotel means limited service in the event of problems. As we were getting ready for bed about 10pm, we noticed a leak from one of the ceiling tiles directly above the shower. The leak quickly became a steady stream, and the ceiling tile looked like it could give way at any moment, dumping who knows what on our heads in the shower. We contacted the front desk and the clerk on duty came up to examine. He said that the manager would be coming to speak with us about changing rooms, but we never did see the manager. And since it was so late, there was no maintenance person available. There was only one other room available which was smaller than what our cruise stateroom was! So at 11pm, we had to move all of our stuff down the hall to another room, in which we and our luggage barely fit. We were offered a reduction in our room rate. The continental breakfast was average. We were allowed to leave our luggage after checkout while we went on a walking tour of Old San Juan. The luggage was put in the main lobby hallway with a locked chain around it. Not what I was expecting when I had gotten confirmation that our luggage could be put in storage. I would not stay at this hotel again.

<Author>yannazmom
<Content>Location is Key! I read the reviews here first and they are very accurate! If you want an economy hotel in the heart of Old San Juan within walking distance of the historic sites, numerous restaurants, shops, etc....this is it! Not a great hotel for kids though....not much for them to do and the kids TV channel was not working well.The room is small, and rather comfy. The bathroom is tiny. The main areas were not air conditioned except for the lobby. The room had A/C but only off or on! No temperature adjustment so it was either COLD, or HOT. I was sick so this created a problem for my chest cold. It is a bare bones, basic room. No frills here but it is clean and the maids are excellent! You may need to ask for washcloths (we had to).We only used the rooftop restaurant for the continental breakfast which consisted of toast, apples, bananas, juices, coffee, milk, cold cereal and some pastries. The view from the roof is not as beautiful as the pics on the site. There is a lot of construction going on and decrepit rooftops nearby.The streets and sidewalks are narrow and cobbled so wear sneakers....sandals may get you a twisted ankle. The area is very easy to navigate and the hotel is a 5 minute walk from the bus station to go to the other cities. We went to Condado beach. It was beautiful, clean, warm.....best part of the vacation. We went to El Morro, San Cristobal (forts), and the gardens of Casa Blanca. It was beautiful! Take sunscreen and water on these walks (within walking distance of the hotel)! Restaurants are plenty and very good! You must go to El Jibarito on Calle del Sol. Very tasty, inexpensive and local. We also tried Barrachina on Fortaleza St (same as Milano). Pricier but great food and service! Fri and Sat nights have a flamenco show there. See the Le Lo Lai show if you are there when it takes place. Ask the front desk cause this show travels and it is well worth it! Parrot Club Restaurant is also near Milano but it was a little more commercial, still good though. Cafe Puerto Rico is around the corner from Milano and has tasty appetizers.The wait for a bus can be 20-40 minutes but the rides are only 75 cents versus a $10-12 cab ride.Great location/convenience but if you want more style and ammentities, you may want to go elsewhere.  
<Date>Dec 13, 2006

<Author>DrRhythm
<Content>Great Deal This is a great deal in the heart of Old San Juan. We wanted to spend part of our stay in Puerto Rico in Old San Juan, and didn't want to break the bank. This place was a good find, and the price is great. The rooms are pretty standard. The location, however, turned out to be the highlight. It is on Calle Fortaleza, which is now considered the SoFo district of Old San Juan. This area is in the middle of all the action, with Calle Fortaleza being filled with great restaurants and bars for night life. We would spend the day exploring and sight seeing, head to the Milano for a quick shower, and we'd then have a whole host of options for dinner. The staff were nice and it was quiet. There is a rooftop restaurant (I think it was called 'Panorama') where you could sit for drinks and look out on the rooftops of Old San Juan. It's not the greatest view, but it was nice to sit there in the open air. Overall a great value if you want to stay in the middle of the action in Old San Juan.

<Author>zjtravel
<Content>Best Cheap Lodging in Old San Juan Hotel Milano is a steal. Located directly in Old San Juan, this property offers clean rooms, friendly staff, and a great location. When staying here, you are within 1-10 min walking distance of amazing restaurants, great shopping, and the cruise departure ports. We saved a lot of mony because we didn't have to take cabs or taxis to and from dinner. Yes the room provided the bare minimum but they are extremely clean. One aspect we were slightly unhappy with were the bed sizes. We got a queen sized bed--which was more like a full size bed. It was ok for a hotel bed--but I have definitly had a more comfortable sleep. But considering it's $50-150 less than the average Old San Juan hotel, I can handle it for one night. So if you are needing a room before or after your cruise or just want to stay in San Juan for one night this hotel is for you!

<Author>Michael-Munich
<Content>Good location, clean, secure and great Puerto Rican Cooking The Hotel is very well located. I loved my daily evening strolls to the harbour (about 4 mins.) to look at the gigantic cruise ships. The open plaza in front of Banco Popular is a must see on weekends. Local musicians, souvenir stands, horse carriage rides ... Within 100 yards from the Milano are many HIP restaurants, bistros and bars, the meeting place of the local Yuppie-Scene.All other tourist attractions of the Old City are within walking distance as well. Just remember to walk slowly and on the shaded side of the street in summer!This was my 3rd or 4th stay in the MILANO during the past 5 years. The staff was friendly as ever, the rooms clean and security good.The Panorama Restaurant on the top floor is one of my favourite dining places because of its tasty home style Puerto Rican Cooking and the good view. My favourites are the Churasco Steak and the Shrimps in spicy red souce (can't remember the exact name). If you are lucky you will meet the owner, Mr. Emeterio, an author and very interesting person to talk to.

<Author>sfltraveler
<Content>great location but dated rooms The location for this hotel is it's best selling point.It is in the heart of the restaurant and shopping area, and walking distance to the rest of old san juan.The lobby is very nice. The rooms are very dated, you must be prepared for that--worn carpets, old bedspreads--but clean. So don't go expecting more or you will be disappointed.The front room had a nice big window and was fine as far as noise since the a/c drowns it out. (ask for a/c controller at desk to adjust a/c, from room you can only turn it on and off)Staff was helpful and friendly. We were disappointed that the rooftop restaurant was closed for vacation so we didn't get to try it.If you're looking for elegance or romance, El Convento would be the place. If you're looking for a more reasonably priced place to lay your head, Milano is a good choice. ADVICE IN OFF SEASON-call before going to restaurants, many are closed, as was the Parrot Club, so you don't waste your time walking around town aimlessly!

<Author>Dog-man
<Content>A good place to sleep in a convenient location This is an uninspiring but acceptable hotel in a great location. Old San Juan does not seem to have a lot of room offerings, so for the price, like the other reviews, Hotel Milano is a great deal. We had 2 parents and 2 kids in two beds on the top floor. Noise was not a problem, the room was clean and, once we got the A/C cranked up, comfortable.The LOCATION -- block and a half from the Parrot Club, Aqua Viva, Dragon Fly conglomerate. Very easy walking distance to all the San Juan sights. See El-Moro at night, and get lost among the colonial buildings and in the cobble-stone streets of Old San Juan. We never felt unsafe, but watch your belongings as Puerto Rico has a reputation for thievery. (Although in our two weeks throughout the island, we NEVER had anything stolen.)

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>location, location, location In the heart of Old San Juan, a short walk to just about everything. A number of highly rated and very good restaurants within 2 blocks and close to shopping, harbor and sights in this unique historical and totally fascinating area. We live in the French Quarter in New Orleans so we really appreciated being in the middle of Old San Juan. Hotel Milano is not fancy but very charming, comfortable, clean, well maintained, etc. Owner and the staff are very friendly and helpful. A simple, self- service breakfast as well as lunch and dinner are served in the Panorama Restaurant on the top floor. We had a very good meal there sampling some nice wine and Puerto Rican specialities. We were so glad we did not stay in the high-rise beach area as we would have been totally bored. It is easy to take a cab to the beaches for the day. We plan on staying there again in the future.

<Author>WorldTraveller65
<Content>Convenient Location Hotel Milano is a historic hotel located conveniently in Old San Juan. We originally booked a standard room, but when we got there we were surprised that the room only had 2 small block type windows located just below the ceiling which were unable to be opened. It felt like we had walked into a cave. We immediately asked for another room, which was an upgrade, but well worth the extra $20. Apparently the front rooms have windows, but are on the front side of the building facing the street so reportedly have a tendency to be noisy. The noise was limited and really didn't bother us since we were in Old San Juan and some noise is to be expected. The service was definitely noteworthy. Miguel was extremely helpful on all levels from changing our room to helping us navigate around the city. Don't expect an extravagant breakfast, though. The included continental breakfast consists of a choice of white or wheat toast, apples or bananas, juice, and coffee. Nevertheless, if you are looking for a hotel with more character than the typical chain hotel and want to be located right in the heart of Old San Juan, Hotel Milano is definitely the place to stay.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Hotel Milano was great! We stayed at the Hotel Milano in Old San Juan pre and post cruise in May 2006 and found it to be great. Juan (the owner) was quick to answer all emails and set up a reservation. The hotel is close to everything in Old San Juan and the rooms are very nice- good size, and everything works - the tv, ac, modern bath and refrigerator. Juan did promise a back room for both reservations and when we arrived for the second they gave us a front room and would not change it (Juan was not there at the time). Since it is on a busy street, the noise woke us up at 2:40 am that night. So we recommend insisting on a back room if you go to bed before that time!The free continental breakfast on the rooftop open restaurant is great - a good start to the day and a good view. Definitely would recommend this hotel and go back there any time.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Charming little hotel We stayed at the Hotel Milano in Old San Juan for 2 nightsin May and found it to be the perfect base for all the thingswe wanted to see in San Juan. The staff is very courteous and helpful, the rooms are spotless,and though they're not fancy, the rooms have nice little amenitieslike a small fridge with bottled water (not marked $3.50 a bottle,as in American chain hotels!). There is a very European feel to this little place that we felt at home in and loved. The included breakfast is a generouscontinental one -- very nice.A big bonus to staying at the Hotel Milano is that you are just1-1/2 blocks from 2 trolley stops, which means you don'tneed a car in Old San Juan (I can't imagine driving thosenarrow streets anyway!). The trolley is free and takes youto all the major historical sights in Old San Juan. Veryconvenient!Another bonus to this hotel is that some of the top restaurantsin all of Puerto Rico are within 2 or 3 blocks! We enjoyedAMAZING meals just steps from our rooms.Especially if you are mainly or solely interested in Old SanJuan and not so much the new part, Hotel Milano isa wonderful choice!

<Author>LAladybug
<Content>Best value as compared to others in the area. I attended a wedding in Old San Juan where guests stayed one of four places. For the price, you really can't beat Hotel Milano. As compared to the HoJo, the rooms were enormous and we had the luxury of a tub! Yes, the hotel is in the middle of the party district and we could hear the music until the wee hours of the morning, but it really wasn't that bad on the 3rd floor. There are four floors of rooms at Milano. The breakfast was just OK, but it was free; I'm not complaining. The rooftop restaurant lured other wedding guests more than once for the wonderful view. After eating at a variety of restaurants, I can honestly say that the hotel's rooftop restaurant has some of the best food in the city and, by far, the best pina coladas! Be sure to try the calamari, seafood paella, and cream soup, too. The location is wonderful as you are in walking distance from the harbor, historic fort, numerous shops... and the free trolly is just a block away on Fortaleza. The Hotel ElConvento and Intercontinental (on Isle Verde beach) were much more upscale, but three times the price. Email me with questions if you so desire. I'll post photos later on. Anita

<Author>mickey3361
<Content>Great Little Secret We stayed for two days, March 25th and 26th, as a stop off before our cruise on Royal Caribbean. The hotel is right smack in the heart of Old San Juan, with wonderful restaurants and shops. We found that our room was clean and a very good value considering the alternatives. We were traveling with another couple who upgraded to a suite fronting on the road while we previously had read a TripAdvisor review and requested and got a room toward the rear of the hotel. Although our view was crappy, there was no noise of revelers on the street at night. Sheets were clean and the hotel staff takes pride in keeping their hotel spiffy. The hotel has a fabulous bar (hey guys, get some port wine next time, will ya!) on the roof top which gave one a view of the Old Town area and the sea in the disdance (harbor area). The front desk clerk was a bit of a sour puss, so management might want to entertain getting someone with a little personality. The porter was great...very helpful with luggage. I would defintely stay here again. The hotel has a restaurant as well, but we didn't try it. Although they serve a continental breakfast, it is a little on the cheapo side in terms of offerings, but at least it was something to get you going in the morning....

<Author>JerryMadison
<Content>Great Location, OK room The Hotel Milano has an absolutely great location if you must stay in Old San Juan. It was a 5-10 minute walk to the ferry and a 15 minute walk to El Morro. A walk in any direction has interesting things to see and I felt safe walking at all times of the day. The rooms are pretty basic. You are definitely paying a premium for staying in Old San Juan. The free breakfast served on the rooftop consisted of cereals, bananas, juices and packaged sweet rolls. I was able to park on the street in front of the hotel...but I was very lucky in that regard. There is ramp parking near the water about 3 blocks away. The staff is friendly and helpful. I would only recommend the hotel if staying in San Juan is a must.....still I think the hotel offers good value considering the great location and other hotel prices nearby.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>location, location, location Our family of 4 stayed at the Hotel Milano in Old San Juan Puerto Rico. It was wonderful. A perfect place when you are spending the day shopping and touring Old San Juan. Much less expensive than El Convento and right in the middle of Old San Juan. The room was great and the roof top bar was lots of fun. Security during daytime and night time is perfect. Our room faced the street, which was a bit party like till 4am on a Friday morning, but with the air conditioning on and the window closed, it barely proved a problem. If you wish, you could have a room at the back of the hotel with less of the outside noise. What we really loved about it was that during the middle of shopping, we were just a 5 minute walk away from our hotel. There are parking lots nearby to park your car, but as we had rented one for our trip, we left it at AVIS at the airport and took a taxi in. There is no or little street parking in Old San Juan and it is much easier to have a taxi drop you off and pick you up. We would certainly stay there again.

<Content>Hotel Milano San Juan - Decent Deal We stayed at the Hotel Milano for 1 night and booked the smallest room for $90, which has no windows. The room was clean and adequate. But again, very clean.The only problem we had was you couldn't control the temperature of the A/C. All other hotels were going for 3 times as much, as other reviewers have pointed out. It's in a great location, very convenient to walk around in Old San Juan. <Author>going2pr
<Content>Excellent location for OSJ and Isla Verde Airport! We stayed at Hotel Milano January 27 and it was a great choice for our one-night stay, before going on to Vieques. The location is excellent for exploring OSJ and the best choice for its proximity to Isla Verde airport!Even tho the website said a minimum of two-nights, they allowed our reservation for just one night. I confirmed availability over email and we called in with our credit card over the phone. They were very responsive via email. When I wrote later for a recommendation for a nearby restaurant to celebrate my birthday, Juan extended a bottle of red wine at the restaurant at the top of the building. As mentioned, the breakfast was basic, but you can't go wrong with a little juice, fruit, toast  cereal to start the day!Our room was a rear, inside and it was a handicap room so the bathroom was large. I've seen other posts about inside rooms with no windows, but ours had three small ones. We, too, heard the thump, thump, thump of a nearby club during the evening. Had we not been so exhausted by our travel and walk around OSJ, we would have been THERE instead of tucked in for the night! So no complaints from us on that. The location was excellent and we were particularly pleased that is so close to Isla Verde airport. About a 10 minute taxi for $12. We paid $15 to get there from SJU.By the way, I highly recommend flying out of Isla Verde to Vieques or whatever other destination served from this airport. You can go to flickr and search for viequesairlink for a few photos from our flight--sorry we don't have any of the Milano!Wishing you safe and fun travel!!

<Content>Delightful Old San Juan hotel We have just returned from a cruise out of San Juan and had booked the Milano Hotel for 2 nights prior to boarding our ship.The hotel has great ambience-clean-large rooms-good air conditioning. Elevator to the 4th floor.It has a great restaurant on the 5th floor-we intended to just have one meal there but ended up having all our meals here.A great menu-interesting scenery-excellent food and delightful staff.Walk out the front door and there are neat shops where ever you turn. <Author>claudinem
<Content>Good for a short stay if you'll just sleep there We just came back from PR, we spent our first two days in Rincon, and then went to San Juan on a Saturday to meet up with friends for a day and a half (they were leaving on a cruise Sunday). We did not want to spend a lot of money for a hotel, since we knew we wouldn't be in the room at all. We had been told when we made the reservations that all they had left was one room with a full-size bed, on the smoking floor. We took it (after being assured that the room wouldn't reek of cigarettes), as we were really happy to have found this hotel for under $100 when everything else in San Juan was going for double. We figured for one night, we could deal with the full-size bed. After having stayed there, I feel one night is the most we could have dealt with. The room was clean, but it was very small, had no windows (they had not told us that), and the AC was weak. There was a hint of cigarette smell, but we didn't feel that it reeked. I am sure every room is different, though, and some probably do reek. So long story short, I have to say, for the amount of time we spent in the room, it was really nice when we checked out and only had to lay out $98. Would we go back? Only if we were facing a similar situation, and were going to use the hotel to sleep and shower. I do think it's probably better than some of the other inns and small hotels I read about.

<Author>Lorenzoe
<Content>Great Value but 4 Stars for value, 2 stars for comfort We stayed at the Milano for two nights on a weekend in Feb. '05. This hotel is a good value if you want to be in Old San Juan. The room was adequate and clean enough and you can't beat the price in Old town. The included breakfast was subpar (they were out of juice, bread, etc.) but we didn't stay there for that reason and there's lots of weekend street noise.Two things you should know:1. If you're not a smoker, make sure they don't put you on the smoking floor 'cause it reeks! They originally gave us a smoking room even though I specifically reserved 'non'. They did switch rooms for us but you should confirm this when you book and again just before arrival.2. This being San Juan on a weekend, there was a LOT of drunken street noise, sounds of bottles breaking in the street, horns and car alarms blasting, etc. until sometime after whenever the bars closed. Ask for an inside room if you want to sleep!

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Great value, outstanding staff - seek out the owner! If you are looking for luxury accommodations, look elsewhere. If you want to support a boutique urban hotel that has heart and soul personified by the charming owner - Juan Emeterio, then this is the place for you in Old San Juan.Emailed the hotel giving them a heads up it was a special trip (10th wedding anniversary and wife's birthday). Juan took the initiative and arranged for a lovely dinner at the rooftop restaurant, complete with wine and a very nice chocolate cake brought in from outside. Juan also joined us 鈥?both the food and the company were treats.Juan can often be seen loading luggage for guests or at the front desk helping out when the staff are busy. Very nice to see this kind of personal touch, so rare today.The rooms are comfortable, convenient to everything. It _is_ an urban hotel, so depending on your location, you may hear things from the street at night - that to me is part of the charm.I get to travel all over the world on business, and will always seek out places like Hotel Milano whenever I can. Juan is a big part of that. Ask for him and say hello if you can - you won't be disappointed.

<Author>ovsiovitch
<Content>Had a Wonderful Time at Hotel Milano We recently spent a few days at Hotel Milano and were well taken care of by Juan San Emeterio and his staff. The hotel is in a beautiful old building. The rooms are not lavish, but comfortably furnished (we came to see Old San Juan, not a hotel room). More important, to me at least, the rooms were immaculate. I've stayed at many large chain hotels that weren't kept as clean as the room here was. We had a wonderful dinner at the Panorama roof top restaurant, and we enjoyed the mornings we went up there for the continental breakfast (the only downside to the continental breakfast is that you would miss going around the corner to Mallorca for breakfast). The hotel is conveniently located to all of the sights and experiences of Old San Juan. San Cristobal is just a short walk from the hotel. El Morro is a little further away, but can be walked. If you want to shop, there are plenty of opportunities (talk to the staff at the front desk they'll tell you who to talk to in some of the stores). The hotel staff was helpful recommending dinner suggestions (there are some great restaurants nearby - though do eat at the hotel too), and in setting up additional travel arrangements to see other parts of Puerto Rico (a trip to El Yunque, transportation to Fajardo). On my return to Old San Juan (which hopefully will be soon) I will return to Hotel Milano.  
<Date>Nov 17, 2005

<Content>delightful ambience We recently spent six days in Old San Juan and staying at the Milano made it particularly pleasant. If you like fine old hotels, this is your cup of tea. It is convenient to reasonable parking (and on-street parking for the diligent) and a perfect starting point for strolling around the old city, which is a delight to the eye.It is also convenient to the cruise ship facilities.Concierge staff was helpful and professional. <Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>A great small hotel We stayed at the Hotel Milano twice, for three days at the front end and a day at the back end of a Caribbean cruise, and loved it. We wanted to stay in Old San Juan for the sightseeing, colors, and history, and were glad to find a small, local, friendly hotel right in the heart of it all. Hotel Milano's location in the middle of Old San Juan was perfect--everything from historical sights to night clubs and great restaurants are within easy walking distance. The hotel staff are very friendly and helpful, the rooftop restaurant is comfortable, and the food is good. We had a front room overlooking Forteleza Street, which was just fine, ample but not luxurious. This is not a chain hotel, which we try to avoid on trips, and we were glad to find a small, friendly, locally owned and operated hotel in the heart of everything. Hotel Milano fit the bill for us, twice. Old San Juan really rocks until the very wee hours on weekends, so some may find the noise from nearby clubs bothersome, but we didn't mind. In fact, one of the waiters in the restaurant was so friendly and nice to us that he asked us to join him and his girl friend for a night out at a really great night club after he got of work! You'd never find that at a big chain or resort hotel. Would I stay there again? Without a doubt and with no misgivings.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Beyond the call of duty! We had stayed at the Hotel Milano in Old San Juan several times. We became acquainted with Mr. Emeterio, the owner, and had spent some time with him in his hotel restaurant on the top floor overlooking the bay. It was a memorable experience.My family and I had decided to organize a banquet to honor my mother in her old age. She lived in Arecibo, Puerto Rico at the time. Because of logistics and family considerations we decided to have the banquet in Orlando, Florida. I did not know, (from the state of Texas where we live), how we were going to have my (wheel chair) mother travel to Orlando with her husband (asthmatic) without some very personal assistance. I decided to call Mr. Emeterio of the Hotel Milano because I just did not know who to turn to.What an awesome decision that turned out to be! We were just astounded at the intense personal interest Mr. Emeterio expressed and how he engaged the whole situation. He employed his staff and his personal driver to have our mother and her husband transported from Arecibo to Old San Juan, put up in his hotel overnight for rest, provided them personal room service, and the following day had them taken to the airport, take care of their paperwork and arranged to have them wheeld to the plane. This is what I call: Beyond the call of duty!.My sincere thanks to Mr. Emeterio and his staff for superior personal service. We will never forget it!tony  anna vera, dallas, texas

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>just what i needed I am currently looking over the balcony at san juan and the cruise ships, listening to some great music in the Panorama bar. Hotel Milano has been a wonderful week. HANDS DOWN I will stay here again if I am visiting Puerto Rico. The staff has been more than friendly (we have dropped off our laptops to the front desk every morning, and every afternoon when we walk back in they hand it to us with a smile). housekeeping has been amazing, I asked for a couple more towels and she actually went to the dryer and got me fresh hot ones instead of the ones that were folded on her cart. And even the owner Juan has been amazing. Would not expect to see him working the front desk, but there he has been. I honesly have no complaints about this place. you read here that some people comment that the staff isnt friendly (they are) or that its to loud (it isnt, but if it is, its becuase you are in old san juan.). and if there is a problem, talk to Juan or anyone else. If you are looking for a nice comfortable hotel in the middle of san juan, with clubs and bars withing stumbling distance, this is the place to go. if you are looking for a place in old san juan, with historical monuments within walking distance, this is the place to go. If you are looking for a place with a bunch of rude faceless employees, a manager who just takes your money at check in, that you will end up paying 200 a night for, this is not the place to go. I was worried when i saw the price, trying to figure out how it can be nice and cheap. its cuz its comfy. the bed was nice, the water was hot, and the mini fridge was great (could use a few microwaces in the halls somewhere, thats about it) and you are getting MORE than you paid for. this type of boutique would run you a mint in the states. only thing, if you want to go to the beach, make sure you walk the half-mile to the bus stop, this is Old San Juan, not Isla Verde or the other beaches. This is historical and party. I love it, and will be coming back again and staying right here.Make sure while you are here, you talk with Juan. Wonderful guy, and read some of his stories (they are in each room).

<Author>kdruschel
<Content>A Sleepless Night in San Juan I honestly can't see why this hotel has gotten such great reviews. It was the right location - in the heart of Old San Juan and up the street from some fabulous restaurants (try Aguaviva!) - but the rooms are dingy and run-down, and all the rooms in the front of the hotel are directly above a pounding disco. It got started around 11pm and didn't stop until well after 4am - we know because it kept us awake the entire time. As for the rooftop restaurant, the food was merely okay, and service was quite poor. The view was mainly of a coal hill across the harbor. Next time, I'll try another location in Old San Juan.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Great treatment, accomodations at Hotel Milano The day we arrived for our honeymoon, planning to spend a night in Old San Juan's Hotel Milano before catching our cruise ship, I left my camera in the cab.The man at the desk very kindly took our stub (hotels are arranged for by a central dispatcher at the airport), got the name of the cab company and contacted them, assuring us he'd do his best to get it back and suggesting we enjoy our limited time in Old San Juan.We checked into our room. No view but clean, with a porter taking our bags. The porter was every bit as considerate and positive as the man at the desk, and wished us a good day.The cabbie returned the camera to the airport, we were happy to find out from the man behind the front desk later that day when we returned. We were thrilled when the man called the airport for us and asked for the camera to be dropped off at the hotel, and they agreed.We took off for dinner and a walking tour of downtown, the waterfront and the information/free rum drink(s) center, and returned to have our camera back!Not only were the room clean and the sheets soft, the air conditioning was blasting cool air out by the time we got in. So much so, we had to turn it down in the middle of the night.The Milano staff considerately suggested tours we might like and assured us it was safe to walk throughout old San Juan, which it proved to be. The next morning we enjoyed the continental breakfast in their rooftop restaurant, enjoying great views of water, a cruise ship in harbor and the rooftop life of that gorgeous, vastly restored and colorful city.I can't say enough things about the impression the employees and accomodations made on me. The closest thing to a negative I can come up with is that there's was no view from our room, just walls of nearby buildings.When we were ready to leave, the morning lobby staff volunteered to chain our bags after we checked out, to make the most of our last few hours before catching the cruise ship. We took advantage of the offer and came back to find our bags safe and sound, and headed off to our honeymoon cruise!A room with a queen size will cost us $85.50 plus $77.0 room tax. Well wortht, too!

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Undeserved Hype - this is like a budget Holiday Inn! I honestly don't understand how this hotel has received such glowing reviews. This hotel is on par with what you would expect if you paid $39.99 for any roadside hotel in the US. Actually, maybe not even that decent.When we stayed at the Hotel Milano it was very hot outside. The lobby felt great; the A/C was on high. However, when we got to our room we realized that the only place in the building with constant A/C is the lobby. The rest of the hotel was very hot and stuffy. Each room has its own A/C unit, but ours was just moving around hot air until we called down to complain. In response to our call, the man at the front desk said he would send up a remote that would make the room cooler - well, he did just that! We had to walk to the elevator closest to our room, and when the doors opened, there lay the remote, by itself, on the floor of the empty elevator. We had to use that remote to make our A/C blow cold air, and then ship it back down to the front desk using the same empty-elevator technique. Hardly 4 star service! And at that our room was still not as cool as we would have liked.Aside from that, the alarm clock is bolted down to the bedside table as if theft is a regular occurrence, the bathroom is 100 degrees since there is no central air, and the street below is noisy - we heard people partying until 3 am outside. The breakfast the next morning is free, and the rooftop deck area is pretty. But the free breakfast, again, is basic at best. Cereal that you eat directly from the plastic container, juice, toast you can make yourself if you choose to, and oranges, apples and bananas in a bowl. Sufficient, but definitely not excellent or above average - I honestly have no clue as to how a hotel that charges almost $100/night in the middle of hurricane season gets such great reviews for such lousy services and accommodations.  
<Date>Sep 19, 2005
