<Content>Loved it! My husband and I stayed at the hotel for only one night, but we were in Old San Juan for two whole days. We were staying there before our cruise left out that Sunday evening. I would definately recommend it to anyone who visits San Juan. The hotel is out of the way of the hustle and bustle of the traffic near the airport.

<Author>bono9763
<Content>Wonderful little hotel We stayed here at the beginning and ending of our cruise (2 nights before and 1 after) in August 2005. It was the perfect location to launch a walking tour of Viejo San Juan (the old city.) The hotel was always close and provided a welcome respite from the heat and humidity. The room was pleasant, the staff was very friendly and helpful, and the complimentary continental breakfast was served on the top floor dining room, whose patio had a marvelous view of the bay. This hotel is not very far from the airport, about 15 minutes, and the price of the room was very reasonable compared to fancier ones in the area. We loved being able to walk along the city wall at night and join in the festivities with many of the local residents, who seem to come here on weekends to stroll the streets, enjoy the music and taste the local treats. It was also close to the ferry, which took us to Catano and Hato Rey for a view of the bay. We would definitely come back here for our next trip to San Juan.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>A Small, Lovely Place in a Lovely City The perfect no-frills hotel right in the middle of Old San Juan, Hotel Milano is located on Calle Fortaleza, within walking distance to everything. You can see the entire old city in one day by foot, two days if you must go down every little winding cobblestone street, like I do. I stayed in a small room facing Fortaleza Street for $125 per night in July, which is off season. This is what I got for my money: air conditioning, a large window, cable TV, a small refrigerator, plenty of closet space, a bathroom with shower stall and a queen bed. The hotel restaurant is on the rooftop and overlooks the city and the bay. All guests are entitled to a free continental breakfast. You can get rooms with smaller beds, without windows or with windows facing the back of the building for amounts ranging from $80 to $115 off season. I found the staff to be very friendly and considerate. There is some room for improvement, however, and I have the following suggestions for the management:1) The lighting in my room was poor. It was difficult for me to read in bed or anywhere in the room, and I love to read. The four lamps had bulbs which gave poor light, and there was no overhead light. 60 watt bulbs (frosted) should be used in all lamps. 2) The air conditioner has no temperature control. In the on position, the room became quite cold. I had to shut the air off and on constantly to control the temperature. 3) The lobby is freezing. I find this to be a problem in many hotels, not just this one. Although I was in San Juan in July, it did rain, and sometimes the weather was warm, not exceeding hot.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Clean, affordable rooms. Honest and courteous staff. We stayed a night at the Hotel Milano on our way to the British Virgin Islands. The room was clean and cool (important for June in the Caribbean). We had dinner at the hotel's rooftop restaurant. The view was great, there was a nice, cool breeze and the food was good.We left a camera in our room and realized it while we were at the San Juan airport. We called the hotel and asked them if they had the camera, and they did. They said they would mail it to our home. It actually made it home before we did. We sincerely appreciate the Hotel Milano's professionalism in dealing with our camera that we left behind. The hotel is in the heart of Old San Juan. It was convenient to shopping and site seeing. It is also convenient to night life. I read that Puerto Ricans love the nightlife and I can confirm from hearing the nightlife well into the morning that this is true. Again, I appreciate the professionalism of the staff at the Hotel Milano. I would stay there again.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Unexpected pleasure in the heart of Old San Juan If you want to stay in a small boutique hotel in the heart of Old San Juan, the Hotel Milano is the place for you! We only stayed a day or so before we boarded a cruise (a short taxi ride away), but really loved being able to walk around, come back for a cool rest or drink, go back out, etc. The rooms aren't overly glamorous, but they're definitely fine. We were in an inside room, which I think might be better because of city night noise (bars, etc.). With the tall ceiling and little ventilation window, it didn't seem inside at all. The best part is the roof-top restaurant bar. Very relaxed; we would go up there just to sit, or maybe order a drink...or have a whole meal. Whatever we wanted to do was fine with the staff. The whole hotel just has a lot of character, the owner is a fascinating person to talk to, the mini-grand lobby is a wonderful eclectic mix of classic elements, modern art and relaxed Puerto Rico. If this is the kind of place you're looking for, you'll like it.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Convenient Hotel We stayed at the Hotel Milano. This is one of the better hotels in Old San Juan because it is close to everything. We went there on our honeymoon. The accommodations were well taken care of. All of the staff was exceptionally nice. Everything was in walking distance which made this the ideal place to be. They were able to book us an excursion to the El Yunque Rain Forest that picked us up and brought us back to the hotel. The tour guide was friendly and knowledgeable. Our room was on the second floor in the front. There was some noise on the weekends but that was expected for being in that part of the district. The pictures of the roof-top restaurant on the hotel's website are real. What a beautiful view of the harbor! We enjoyed our time there in spite of the little noise we experienced. We recommend this hotel to anyone going to Puerto Rico and staying in San Juan.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>a hidden delight! We just returned from a 7-day vacation in Puerto Rico. What a pleasant surprise we experienced! We made the choice to stay in Historical Old San Juan. We found this wonderful small hotel called Hotel Milano right in the middle of the city. The price was right, the rooms were comfortable and very clean, the staff was professional and vey accommodating, the food from their own 5th floor resaurant with harbor views was superior and the bonus was their little surprising specialties that they would make for you. We were able to walk to all points of Old San Juan from this hotel and enjoy the sights, the shops, the art galleries, other restaurants and not have to walk for miles to get back to our room. I wish we had found this place sooner. Old San Juan is like a city in old Spain re-created.We were fearful of the potential disappointments and the disasters that some experience with vacations, but this was a pleasant stay and most certainly a hidden delight just waiting for those looking for such a romantic little spot in this planet. Von voyage! From Dallas.

<Author>lanacaine
<Content>Good choice in Old SJU I stayed two nights at the Milano 31 March-2 April. The hotel is very centrally located with nothing more than a ten to fifteen minute walk; the staff were friendly and helpful. While not a luxury property, it is a good choice for anyone on a budget or who enjoys a smaller hotel. Fortaleza at night is truly noisy; a room in the back will help if you are a light sleeper.Complimentary continental breakfast (fruit and cereal) is served every AM in Panorama, the hotel's rooftop restaurant; lunch or dinner is reasonable and easy if you're in the hotel and a little too tired to hit the hotspots down the street.

<Author>Erika_V
<Content>Convenient hotel, friendly, helpful staff, however... We spent two nights here, Monday and Good Friday. Overall, the hotel is clean, safe, very friendly, helpful staff. However, if you want to sleep at all, do not accept a room facing Calle Fortaleza or what they call a front room. The traffic runs right underneath your window, backs up at all hours of the night with horns blaring and such, due to bars and night clubs in the area (one way street leaving Old San Juan just under your window). The noise was not from night clubs, just people out and about. The restraurant on the 4th floor, called Panorama was not too great. I've had worse, but it was expensive and not very flavorful. So many close places within walking distance, but none were open on Good Friday.I would definitely stay here again, with a room not facing the street. You can't beat the convenience to everything, and the price when compared to other hotels in Old San Juan, can not be beat. I felt perfectly safe at the hotel and walking to nearby restaurants in the evening with my husband and yound daughters.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>A Great Stay at the Hotel Milano! (March 2005) This cozy little hotel is perfect for travelers looking for a comfortable, clean place to stay, without all the excessive frills. The only frill is the owner, Juan San Emeterio who is as charming, warm, and friendly as his hotel - we hope you will have the pleasure of meeting him. The hotel is smack in the middle of Old San Juan with its cute cobblestone streets and fabulous restaurants, night clubs, and shops within just a few blocks radius. The hotel has its own roof-top restaurant called The Panorama with a pretty view of the harbor and a nice cool breeze. There, you can enjoy tasty traditional Puerto Rican dishes, refreshing pina coladas, and creamy coconut custard (made on site!). We're excited to share with everyone our discovery of this delightful hotel!

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Great place, great view, right price We could not have been more pleased with the accomodations at Hotel Milano. The location is smack dab in the middle of old San Juan and just steps from great restaurants and shops. The roof top restaurant offered good food and a great view. I am surprised that more restaurants have not opened their roofs to the views and breezes. We especially enjoyed watching the cruise ship we had just disembarked, leave later that night. As many have stated, the rooms were not particularly spacious but certainly the cost and location more than made up for that. They were clean and well attended and very safe. We took the larger queen double located in the front of the hotel and it was large enough for the two of us with all our bags and souvenirs. Although there was a television, don't plan to spend much time watching any favorites as the selction is limited. It was nice after a day of sight seeing or shopping to be able to walk to our room and not have to deal with a taxi or car. (Parking is available in garages but is expensive.) I would recommend this hotel to anyone planning a trip to San Juan, particularly anyone who is cruising out of the city. It is a nice quiet place to begin or end a trip on a ship.  
<Date>Mar 11, 2005

<Author>lilipadk
<Content>Top notch location, and a nice hotel overall. This hotel is right in Old San Juan, as central as can be - 5 to 10 minute walk to either old fort, 2 minutes walk to the Parrot Club and sister restaurants. We opted for the cheapest room which at $100/nt although very small, had all the ammenities, like shampoo, towels, tissues, TV/cable, fridge, wake up calls. I state this becasue none of the other hotels we stayed at for similar prices, or more, had all this. The hotel is also pretty new and spotless (www.hotelmilanopr.com). The location was right in the middle of the old city, 5-10 minute walk to both forts, and 3 minutes to the Parrot Club restaurant. The continental breakfast on the roof top with views of the water was just that, a continental breakfast with toast, donuts, coffee/juice, fruit, cereal and self service. This is a little Marriott in the city w/o the price tag or the extra charges. Just be prepared to share some space or pay a bit more $ for a larger room.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Great Location My daughter found this quaint hotel while touring Old San Juan. It is an ideal location for touring since it is right in the center of the city. We were able to walk everywhere. We had a room in the front since it is the only rooms with large windows. It is well air conditioned and has a refrigerator. The only drawback was no wash cloths (they don't provide them) and no fresh decaf coffee. This was a small price to pay for the friendly staff and comfortable rooms. The restaurant is not available for the handicapped since the elevator does not go to the top floor where it is located. They provided a Continental Breakfast each morning with fresh juice, fruit, cereal, bagels and sweet rolls. The view of the harbor is a plus.If I return to San Juan, I will certainly stay at this hotel.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>DON'T MISS THE MILANO The Milano is a very special hotel, a smallish place nestled in the heart of old San Juan. From some of its rooms there is a glorious view of the port of San Juan, and its rooftop bar and restaurant is an intimate and magical spot at any time of day or evening. But what sets the hotel apart from any other, is its owner and manager, Juan San Emeterio, an extraordinary man, a kind of latter-day Kahlil Gibran. He has written a number of wonderful uplifting spiritual works, and a copy of one of his volumes is left in every room. He will drop everything for a good conversation, and has a natural fascination with people, so that a stay here is a spiritually enlightening experience. The rapturous responses he has received on his website bear witness to the effect a stay at his hotel has had on his clientele. A hotel unlike any other...

<Author>rjrdived
<Content>Old San Juan, St. John and Virgin Gorda Summer Vacation We just returned from a destination wedding trip which we also rolled into a two week summer vacation. The wedding was at the WESTIN Hotel on St. John, USVI, and of course was a wonderful affair. As we did not stay at the hotel, I cannot comment on the facilities except Cruz Bay Watersports, who I dived with, were great. There were approximately 80 guest at the wedding and I heard no complaints about the hotel.The trip started from Houston to Old San Juan Puerto Rico, where we stayed in an a modest hotel, The Hotel Milano on Forteleza St. , right in the middle of Old San Juan. It was very close to the restaurants and as Old San Juan is fairly compact, it made sight seeing easy. The staff was gracious and very helpful. The hotel is not fancy, but we had plenty of room and a BB type breakfast before launching out to see the historical sights which are many and actually easy to see in one day. The restaurants Querencia and another restaurant owned by the Parrot Club restaurant owner was wonderfulThe 3rd day we flew to St. Thomas and caught the ferry to St. John for the wedding festivities, days of snorkeling , lying on the beaches and lazing around at a Cloud Nine Villa Moonsong , a wonderful house for two couples. We overlooked Hart Bay which was about a mile and a half from the Westin which made it easy to get to the wedding functions. The beaches on St. John are really magnificent and if there is an odd cruise ship there in the summer and you want to go to Trunk Bay , just go a little early for the perfect spot on the beach. Water Lemon Cay was our favorite snorkeling beach , but others in the party liked Trunk , Frances Bay and Cinnamon Bays. A bay for everyone. Lunches and dinners at Asolare, Paradiso, Fish Trap, Panini's, The Balcony were all wonderful as was the bar and restaurant outside Low Watersports shop. Stay away from the beach bar next toPanini's as the service is non existent but the food was good. The Bar B Q ribs at Uncle Joes fell off the bones .They were so tender. The people at Cloud Nine Villas were wonderful and sent one all the information needed for an island vacation.If you have not used the ferries to get around , do so as they are reasonable means of transportation. WE took the ferry to West End Tortola, cabbed to Roadtown and then took the ferry to Virgin Gorda. We rented a Suzuki jeep from Mahogany Car Rentals and it was really better than the Jeep ented on St. John. We stayed in a perfect house for two, Casa Luna ,rented through Guavaberry Vacation Homes on Virgin Gorda. It was a 3 minute walk to Spring Bay and The Crawl. The Baths and Devil's Bay are just a short walk or snorkle away. The people at Guavaberry could not have been nicer or more helpful. The house they suggested was perfect for us.The bays, beaches and people on Virgin Gorda are wonderful. The BVI islanders are much friendlier and the pace is not as hectic and driven as in the USVI. We had a wonderful time and would recommend the places we stayed and the restaurants we dined at without reservations. The restaurants on Virgin Gorda are limited. We dined at Georgio's Table overlooking Maho Bay and Pond Bay which was expensive but wonderful. We also ate the the Mine Shaft to listen to Morris Mark and see the senset. It is a great sunset place and has all the correct sunset drinks. The Rock wth its piano player and great food was a surprise. For sheer beauty try the Top of the Baths or for a good sandwich, try Mad Dogs in the same general location. A pizza at the Bath and Turtle was also great.We flew to St. Thomas to return home but to make the plane we overnighted at a local small 12 room hotel, Villa Blanca and had our last dinner at Randy's. The dinner was truly wonderful. The restaurant is also a bistro and wine shop in the hills above Charlotte Amalie, St. Thomas.A great vacationand I would recommend such a trip to anyone who enjoys the swaying palms trees. beautiful water, snorkling and diving, not to mention great meals.Russell Ramsey

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>A Solid 3 star hotel This is a 3 star hotel, nothing more, nothing less--typical if you have traveled in Europe in similar accomodations. Rooms clean, clean towels, decent front desk help. The night attendant was not very helpful, day staff much better. Limited Breakfast--free--but not that great. Coffee was good. Perfect for us because we had a full sightseeing plan and needed a place to shower, clean up and rest. Location is really fantastic, you can walk everywhere from the hotel--shopping and restaurants right at your fingertips. We parked for free near the municipal lot, not inside, although it is very reasonable at $5.00 a day. Car rental is a must if in PR for more than a day. We enjoyed having flexibility in being able to get around (plus we saw more than on foot) and our trip to the rain forest (El Yunque) was excellent--don't miss it, extend your trip if necessary. Tio's Bar and Rest right next to the hotel is a great stop to have a drink--we went every night--great mojitos. Breni, blonde bartender gave us great tips, even helped us find a laundromat--tell her hi from the NY couple looking for a laundromat! El Bombonera, a PRican diner was good fun. Gruff service, but decent and cheap food--lots of locals eat there. El Convento for tapas and sangria was a great dinner alternative. Walking and discovering is the best way to enjoy Old San Juan, having a hotel in the heart of it all is worth it and gives you the flexibility to see as much as possible. Casino a short walk away. If taking a cruise (RC or Princess), avoid going to the pier before 4 or 5pm. The traffic is insane and there is only 1 road that gets you to the Pan American pier. Enjoy Old San Juan!

<Author>mudhen1
<Content>Good times in Old San Juan A buddy and I went to San Juan in 4/04 and stayed at the Hotel Milano. We could not have asked for a better place to stay. It was centrally located to all of Old San Juans attractions and it is on the same block as the city's best restaurants. You could always stay on the beach in Condado or Isla Verde, but you miss out on the character and charm of Old San Juan. Besides, the beach was only a 25 cent bus ride (takes 30 minutes). A cab would run you anywhere from 10-16 dollars to go to the beach. Right around the block from Hotel Milano was Senor Frogs, a really fun party spot any night of the week. We met some beautiful women there and danced and drank all night. Hotel Milano was also close to the pier to catch the boat to Catano to see the Bacardi factory, which is a must see. The hotel is also not far from Calle San Sebastian which throws an amazing block party/street fair the first Tuesday of every month. The hotel is very nice and the staff was very helpful. If you are interested in seeing daylight, make sure you ask for a front room because the back rooms do not have windows. Also the continental breakfast was disappointing. Toast and going bad fruit just did not cut it. Besides that, I would definately stay here again for the convenience and location

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>We were surprised! This hotel is not for the faint of heart. Understand that you get what you pay for. With that said, we had a wonderful experience. The hotel was clean, the staff extremely friendly and helpful and the location could not have been better. The price was one of the most reasonable in San Juan and we took a gamble. It turned out to be worth it. There's nothing better than walking out the front door of your hotel and being in the midst of the streets of Old San Juan. The nightclub on Saturday night was quite loud. Wake up early and walk the few blocks up the hill to El Morro, then walk back to the hotel and watch the streets come alive. We will definitely return to Old San Juan and will plan to stay at Hotel Milano.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Very clean above average 3 star hotel with good sevice It is a really good hotel. They change towels every day, make the bed and clean the room sooo good. The hotel itself really neat. Every day they put a bottle of water in the cooler and put candies on the drawer :-) You should defenately try some seafood at the Panarama restaurant located on the roof. Guys at the reception are very friendly but not very helpful with giving information about the town, you better go to information center which is 3 blocks down. Choice of food for breakfast is limited to toasts coffee and fruits. The location is great, all bars and restaurants are just 2-3 blocks away. People that live in fancy restaurants on the beach come to Old San Juan at nights, because it's absolutely nothing to do around there.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Can't wait to return! After a number of stays in the beachfront Condado and Isla Verde areas, My husband and I decided to spend a week in Old San Juan. We were lucky to find a lovely hotel that was within easy walking distance of all the wonderful historical and cultrural sites. The Hotel Milano reflected the rich vibrant atmosphere of the old city. It was clean ,decorated in soft colors, and furnished with some lovely antiques. The bed was very comfortable after a long day of sight-seeing. There was plenty of storage, a nice bathroom and a good-sized refrigerator. A small market several blocks away kept us supplied with snacks and beverages. The staff was warm and inviting and went out of their way to accomodate my wheelchair needs. Although we know a little Spanish, it was reassuring to know that almost all staff were also fluent in English and made several phone calls for us in Spanish. The rooftop restaurant served delicious food. The complimentary breakfast was a pleasant surprise. We appreciated the personalized service that is missing in the large chain hotels. We look forward to returning soon to a place that really felt like home.  
<Date>Apr 2, 2004

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Wonderful Stay We had a wonderful stay at Hotel Milano. We were there 3 nights (post Cruise) and found that ending our vacation in Old San Juan just topped our vacation (Jan 2004). The front desk staff - met at least 3 of them- all were very friendly  assisted us with phone calls ie) to scuba shops, taxis.. from the front desk/lobby phones. As with other comments on your site, the Location was the best. Shopping and Eating at all hours!! That's a delight. We were adventurous  was able to walk to Fort Morro  Fort Cristobal. Walking a block to take the ferry over to the Barcardi Distillary was also great fun! Free drinks there!!

<Author>darkeyes
<Content>Great location Just spent 5 nights at the Milano. The rooms are small but very clean and the bed was very comfortable. I was upgraded to a room with windows which you have to stand on a chair to look out of and which overlooked the air conditioning units. However, I still found the windows helpful as they only had a few lights with 25 watt bulbs which I found it very difficult to read by. (I finally went out and purchased a 60 watt to work by. )I found the staff to be somewhat indifferent, the food in the top floor restaurant to be very good and the location of the hotel excellent. On Friday and Saturday nights the music from a nearby nightclub actually vibrated the walls and my bed from 10:30 pm to about 3:30 am. At least the music was good.
